drop table area_coordinate;

CREATE TABLE area_coordinate ( 
    area_code CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    lev1 VARCHAR2(25) NOT NULL,
    lev2 VARCHAR2(25),
    lev2_1 varchar2(20),
    lev3 VARCHAR2(25),
    co_X VARCHAR2(3) NOT NULL,
    co_Y VARCHAR2(3) NOT NULL
);
